\doxysubsection*{Macros}
\begin{Indent}\textbf{ Mouse and Keyboard Events}\par
{\em This and the following constants define the non-\/\+A\+S\+C\+II keys on the keyboard for F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD and F\+L\+\_\+\+S\+H\+O\+R\+T\+C\+UT events.

\doxysubsection*{Box Types}
\label{_amgrp2126f69af9d5d7bac9ff67a532026acc}%
F\+L\+TK standard box types

This enum defines the standard box types included with F\+L\+TK.

F\+L\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+B\+OX means nothing is drawn at all, so whatever is already on the screen remains. The F\+L\+\_\+...\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+ME types only draw their edges, leaving the interior unchanged. The blue color in Figure 1 is the area that is not drawn by the frame types.

 
\begin{DoxyImage}
\includegraphics[width=10cm]{boxtypes.png}
\doxyfigcaption{F\+L\+TK standard box types}
\end{DoxyImage}

\doxysubsection*{Alignment Flags}
\label{_amgrpd9d225b55647fd693b298abca33f4418}%
Flags to control the label alignment.

This controls how the label is displayed next to or inside the widget. The default value is F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+L\+I\+G\+N\+\_\+\+C\+E\+N\+T\+ER (0) for most widgets, which centers the label inside the widget.

Flags can be or\textquotesingle{}d to achieve a combination of alignments, but there are some \char`\"{}magic values\char`\"{} (e.\+g. combinations of T\+OP and B\+O\+T\+T\+OM and of L\+E\+FT and R\+I\+G\+HT) that have special meanings (see below). For instance\+:~\newline
 F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+L\+I\+G\+N\+\_\+\+T\+O\+P\+\_\+\+L\+E\+FT == (F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+L\+I\+G\+N\+\_\+\+T\+O\+P$\vert$\+F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+L\+I\+G\+N\+\_\+\+L\+E\+FT) != F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+L\+I\+G\+N\+\_\+\+L\+E\+F\+T\+\_\+\+T\+OP.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{Outside alignments (\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_ade440c90fc9c2495fdf04c9cb34fba34}{FL\_ALIGN\_INSIDE}} is not set):}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{           TOP\_LEFT        TOP       TOP\_RIGHT}
\DoxyCodeLine{           +-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+}
\DoxyCodeLine{   LEFT\_TOP|                                 |RIGHT\_TOP}
\DoxyCodeLine{           |                                 |}
\DoxyCodeLine{       LEFT|             CENTER              |RIGHT}
\DoxyCodeLine{           |                                 |}
\DoxyCodeLine{LEFT\_BOTTOM|                                 |RIGHT\_BOTTOM}
\DoxyCodeLine{           +-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+}
\DoxyCodeLine{           BOTTOM\_LEFT   BOTTOM   BOTTOM\_RIGHT}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{Inside alignments (\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_ade440c90fc9c2495fdf04c9cb34fba34}{FL\_ALIGN\_INSIDE}} is set):}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\doxysubsection*{Colors}
\label{_amgrp5d50889672f6f860d14f502de3de1957}%
 The Fl\+\_\+\+Color type holds an F\+L\+TK color value.

Colors are either 8-\/bit indexes into a \href{fltk-colormap.png}{\texttt{ virtual colormap}} or 24-\/bit R\+GB color values. (See drawing\+\_\+colors for the default F\+L\+TK colormap)

Color indices occupy the lower 8 bits of the value, while R\+GB colors occupy the upper 24 bits, for a byte organization of R\+G\+BI.


\begin{DoxyPre}
 Fl\_Color => 0xrrggbbii
                | | | |
                | | | +-\/-\/-\/ index between 0 and 255
                | | +-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ blue color component (8 bit)
                | +-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ green component (8 bit)
                +-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ red component (8 bit)
 \end{DoxyPre}


A color can have either an index or an rgb value. Colors with rgb set and an index $>$0 are reserved for special use. \begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item 
\#define \mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_aa8fe2e5047a2dd1be37e8336dfca918d}{F\+L\+\_\+\+F\+R\+E\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+OR}}~(\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a8b762953646f8abee866061f1af78a6a}{Fl\+\_\+\+Color}})16

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
This file contains type definitions and general enumerations. 

\doxysubsection{Macro Definition Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_a619cd27e13a15a7b1b5ead0932dd3912}\label{_enumerations_8_h_a619cd27e13a15a7b1b5ead0932dd3912}} 
\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_ABI\_VERSION@{FL\_ABI\_VERSION}}
\index{FL\_ABI\_VERSION@{FL\_ABI\_VERSION}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FL\_ABI\_VERSION}{FL\_ABI\_VERSION}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+B\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON~(\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a10c923db4d613150c8a3937f9775ccd0}{F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+A\+J\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}}$\ast$10000 + \mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a165d2781eff3186354a5f5db0528976d}{F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}}$\ast$100)}

The F\+L\+TK A\+BI (Application Binary Interface) version number as an {\itshape int}.

F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+B\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON is an {\itshape int} that describes the major, minor, and patch A\+BI version numbers in the same format as F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON.

The A\+BI version number {\ttfamily F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+B\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON} is usually the same as the A\+PI version {\ttfamily F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON} with the last two digits set to \textquotesingle{}00\textquotesingle{}.

F\+L\+TK retains the A\+BI (Application Binary Interface) during patch releases of the same major and minor versions. Examples\+:

\begin{DoxyVerb}  FLTK Version  FL_API_VERSION  FL_ABI_VERSION  FL_VERSION (deprecated)
    1.3.0          10300           10300           1.0300
1.3.4          10304           10300           1.0304
\end{DoxyVerb}


Version 1.\+2.\+3 is actually stored as 10203 to allow for more than 9 minor and patch releases.

The F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+A\+J\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON, F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON, and F\+L\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON constants give the integral values for the major, minor, and patch releases respectively.

To enable new A\+B\+I-\/breaking features in patch releases you can configure F\+L\+TK to use a higher F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+B\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
R\+E\+A\+D\+M\+E.\+abi-\/version.\+txt 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+B\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON~\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a53186dc2831a9786ba70657c771871a7}{F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}}}

F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+B\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON is an {\itshape int} that describes the major, minor, and patch A\+BI version numbers in the same format as F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON.

F\+L\+TK retains the A\+BI (Application Binary Interface) during patch releases of the same major and minor versions. Examples\+:

\begin{DoxyVerb}  FLTK Version  FL_API_VERSION  FL_ABI_VERSION  FL_VERSION (deprecated)
    1.3.0          10300           10300           1.0300
1.3.4          10304           10300           1.0304
\end{DoxyVerb}


Version 1.\+2.\+3 is actually stored as 10203 to allow for more than 9 minor and patch releases.

The F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+A\+J\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON, F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON, and F\+L\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON constants give the integral values for the major, minor, and patch releases respectively.

To enable new A\+B\+I-\/breaking features in patch releases you can configure F\+L\+TK to use a higher F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+B\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FL\_API\_VERSION}{FL\_API\_VERSION}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON~(\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a10c923db4d613150c8a3937f9775ccd0}{F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+A\+J\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}}$\ast$10000 + \mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a165d2781eff3186354a5f5db0528976d}{F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}}$\ast$100 + \mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_afc7b82e6fcfbb451d38e8a0cacde302a}{F\+L\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}})}

The F\+L\+TK A\+PI version number as an {\itshape int}.

F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON is an {\itshape int} that describes the major, minor, and patch version numbers.

Version 1.\+2.\+3 is actually stored as 10203 to allow for more than 9 minor and patch releases.

The F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+A\+J\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON, F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+O\+R\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON, and F\+L\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON constants give the integral values for the major, minor, and patch releases respectively.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON is intended to replace the deprecated {\itshape double} F\+L\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON.
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_a94499c96b5f3ca212d90a2c41f947a67}\label{_enumerations_8_h_a94499c96b5f3ca212d90a2c41f947a67}} 
\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_VERSION@{FL\_VERSION}}
\index{FL\_VERSION@{FL\_VERSION}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FL\_VERSION}{FL\_VERSION}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define F\+L\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{              ( (double)\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a10c923db4d613150c8a3937f9775ccd0}{FL\_MAJOR\_VERSION}} + \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{              (\textcolor{keywordtype}{double})\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a165d2781eff3186354a5f5db0528976d}{FL\_MINOR\_VERSION}} * 0.01 + \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{              (double)\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_afc7b82e6fcfbb451d38e8a0cacde302a}{FL\_PATCH\_VERSION}} * 0.0001 )}

\end{DoxyCode}
The F\+L\+TK version number as a {\itshape double}.

F\+L\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON is a {\itshape double} that describes the major, minor, and patch version numbers.

Version 1.\+2.\+3 is actually stored as 1.\+0203 to allow for more than 9 minor and patch releases.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000001}{Deprecated}}]This {\ttfamily double} version number is retained for compatibility with existing program code. New code should use {\itshape int} F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON instead. F\+L\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON is deprecated because comparisons of floating point values may fail due to rounding errors. However, there are currently no plans to remove this deprecated constant.\end{DoxyRefDesc}


F\+L\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON is equivalent to {\itshape (double)F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON / 10000}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl_a691ce8682015fdbd38e49e9257316409}{Fl\+::version()}} (deprecated as well) 

\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a53186dc2831a9786ba70657c771871a7}{F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+I\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}}

\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!Fl\_Cursor@{Fl\_Cursor}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fl\_Cursor}{Fl\_Cursor}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a72bde974edc7926b1217dd51b8c7e8e0}{Fl\+\_\+\+Cursor}}}

The following constants define the mouse cursors that are available in F\+L\+TK.

Cursors are provided by the system when available, or bitmaps built into F\+L\+TK as a fallback.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Todo}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{todo__todo000005}{Todo}}]enum Fl\+\_\+\+Cursor needs maybe an image. \end{DoxyRefDesc}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3}} 
\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!Fl\_Event@{Fl\_Event}}
\index{Fl\_Event@{Fl\_Event}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fl\_Event}{Fl\_Event}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3}{Fl\+\_\+\+Event}}}

Every time a user moves the mouse pointer, clicks a button, or presses a key, an event is generated and sent to your application. Events can also come from other programs like the window manager.

Events are identified by the integer argument passed to the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_a3521aba25eda761620953dd49d335ea7}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::handle()}} virtual method. Other information about the most recent event is stored in static locations and acquired by calling the Fl\+::event\+\_\+$\ast$() methods. This static information remains valid until the next event is read from the window system, so it is ok to look at it outside of the handle() method.

Event numbers can be converted to their actual names using the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_gafae60209182e08e80094cde8905d3521}{fl\+\_\+eventnames}}\mbox{[}\mbox{]} array defined in \#include $<$F\+L/names.\+h$>$

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga6647c55948fe1d8be9367267529e9c54}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+text()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga1ac131e3cd5ca674cc022b1f77233449}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+key()}}, class \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl}{Fl}}\+:\+: 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_NO\_EVENT@{FL\_NO\_EVENT}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_NO\_EVENT@{FL\_NO\_EVENT}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3aee4e8cf3108b1a47c67231451d39042f}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3aee4e8cf3108b1a47c67231451d39042f}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+NT&No event. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_PUSH@{FL\_PUSH}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_PUSH@{FL\_PUSH}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a44972d76423f3e380ae12c36827944e3}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a44972d76423f3e380ae12c36827944e3}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+P\+U\+SH&A mouse button has gone down with the mouse pointing at this widget. You can find out what button by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga7ae6d99ceb1a2afb8a1dc4455ac941cd}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+button()}}. You find out the mouse position by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga91585fcbaa1e79f7452fd2d16a82136e}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+x()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga192a0c5a37f33b9d117a69f20977c2a1}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+y()}}.

A widget indicates that it \char`\"{}wants\char`\"{} the mouse click by returning non-\/zero from its \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_a3521aba25eda761620953dd49d335ea7}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::handle()}} method. It will then become the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_gadcd24382935bf08b56b1532dfe80da25}{Fl\+::pushed()}} widget and will get F\+L\+\_\+\+D\+R\+AG and the matching F\+L\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+E\+A\+SE events. ~\newline
 If \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_a3521aba25eda761620953dd49d335ea7}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::handle()}} returns zero then F\+L\+TK will try sending the F\+L\+\_\+\+P\+U\+SH to another widget. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_RELEASE@{FL\_RELEASE}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_RELEASE@{FL\_RELEASE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a5949b5ff170a8236d2745eddb1e9fd9a}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a5949b5ff170a8236d2745eddb1e9fd9a}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+E\+A\+SE&A mouse button has been released. You can find out what button by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga7ae6d99ceb1a2afb8a1dc4455ac941cd}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+button()}}.

In order to receive the F\+L\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+E\+A\+SE event, the widget must return non-\/zero when handling F\+L\+\_\+\+P\+U\+SH. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_ENTER@{FL\_ENTER}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_ENTER@{FL\_ENTER}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a29b256ac93d443dd33a8c610c24e7af5}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a29b256ac93d443dd33a8c610c24e7af5}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+ER&The mouse has been moved to point at this widget. This can be used for highlighting feedback. If a widget wants to highlight or otherwise track the mouse, it indicates this by returning non-\/zero from its handle() method. It then becomes the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga5b55ce634002a2743c24c4c4db7cbdd4}{Fl\+::belowmouse()}} widget and will receive F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+O\+VE and F\+L\+\_\+\+L\+E\+A\+VE events. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_LEAVE@{FL\_LEAVE}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_LEAVE@{FL\_LEAVE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3aa776cf3129e97140c88a062881a2d29a}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3aa776cf3129e97140c88a062881a2d29a}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+L\+E\+A\+VE&The mouse has moved out of the widget. In order to receive the F\+L\+\_\+\+L\+E\+A\+VE event, the widget must return non-\/zero when handling F\+L\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+ER. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_DRAG@{FL\_DRAG}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_DRAG@{FL\_DRAG}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3aaad5c7b2302d7bfe6c6d37b50b4c70f0}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3aaad5c7b2302d7bfe6c6d37b50b4c70f0}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+D\+R\+AG&The mouse has moved with a button held down. The current button state is in \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_gafa17a5b4d8d9163631c88142e60447ed}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+state()}}. The mouse position is in \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga91585fcbaa1e79f7452fd2d16a82136e}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+x()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga192a0c5a37f33b9d117a69f20977c2a1}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+y()}}.

In order to receive F\+L\+\_\+\+D\+R\+AG events, the widget must return non-\/zero when handling F\+L\+\_\+\+P\+U\+SH. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_FOCUS@{FL\_FOCUS}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_FOCUS@{FL\_FOCUS}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3adaac2a187beb309443d668a20a59986b}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3adaac2a187beb309443d668a20a59986b}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+F\+O\+C\+US&This indicates an {\itshape attempt} to give a widget the keyboard focus.

If a widget wants the focus, it should change itself to display the fact that it has the focus, and return non-\/zero from its handle() method. It then becomes the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga7f0e9836db43268979e0b3a999583b7f}{Fl\+::focus()}} widget and gets F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+D\+O\+WN, F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+UP, and F\+L\+\_\+\+U\+N\+F\+O\+C\+US events.

The focus will change either because the window manager changed which window gets the focus, or because the user tried to navigate using tab, arrows, or other keys. You can check \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga1ac131e3cd5ca674cc022b1f77233449}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+key()}} to figure out why it moved. For navigation it will be the key pressed and for interaction with the window manager it will be zero. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_UNFOCUS@{FL\_UNFOCUS}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_UNFOCUS@{FL\_UNFOCUS}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a7d2e5eb9247b1927ba5cc26dc82acaf3}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a7d2e5eb9247b1927ba5cc26dc82acaf3}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+U\+N\+F\+O\+C\+US&This event is sent to the previous \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga7f0e9836db43268979e0b3a999583b7f}{Fl\+::focus()}} widget when another widget gets the focus or the window loses focus. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_KEYDOWN@{FL\_KEYDOWN}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_KEYDOWN@{FL\_KEYDOWN}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a1d132318f4c72305fd1babbbc4dbeb1a}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a1d132318f4c72305fd1babbbc4dbeb1a}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+D\+O\+WN&A key was pressed (F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+D\+O\+WN) or released (F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+UP). Fl\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD is a synonym for F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+D\+O\+WN. The key can be found in \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga1ac131e3cd5ca674cc022b1f77233449}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+key()}}. The text that the key should insert can be found with \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga6647c55948fe1d8be9367267529e9c54}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+text()}} and its length is in \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga38f2de89fbdf59ad2cd4dca93f472911}{Fl\+::event\+\_\+length()}}. If you use the key handle() should return 1. If you return zero then F\+L\+TK assumes you ignored the key and will then attempt to send it to a parent widget. If none of them want it, it will change the event into a F\+L\+\_\+\+S\+H\+O\+R\+T\+C\+UT event.

To receive F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD events you must also respond to the F\+L\+\_\+\+F\+O\+C\+US and F\+L\+\_\+\+U\+N\+F\+O\+C\+US events.

If you are writing a text-\/editing widget you may also want to call the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga2c16ab49eb753b98f3d8f1e96429d094}{Fl\+::compose()}} function to translate individual keystrokes into non-\/\+A\+S\+C\+II characters.

F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+UP events are sent to the widget that currently has focus. This is not necessarily the same widget that received the corresponding F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+D\+O\+WN event because focus may have changed between events. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_KEYBOARD@{FL\_KEYBOARD}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_KEYBOARD@{FL\_KEYBOARD}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a1387c0430ec873aa44704954a369143b}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a1387c0430ec873aa44704954a369143b}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD&Equivalent to F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+D\+O\+WN. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a1d132318f4c72305fd1babbbc4dbeb1a}{F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+D\+O\+WN}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_KEYUP@{FL\_KEYUP}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_KEYUP@{FL\_KEYUP}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3ab0e1a75a36767b878915e59e5f9e3be8}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3ab0e1a75a36767b878915e59e5f9e3be8}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+UP&Key release event. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a1d132318f4c72305fd1babbbc4dbeb1a}{F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+D\+O\+WN}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_CLOSE@{FL\_CLOSE}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_CLOSE@{FL\_CLOSE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a42828f08af2b2191bbc60e113ec08f01}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a42828f08af2b2191bbc60e113ec08f01}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+C\+L\+O\+SE&The user clicked the close button of a window. This event is used internally only to trigger the callback of \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___window}{Fl\+\_\+\+Window}} derived classed. The default callback closes the window calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___window_a42fbeddb68a203ff9123d33156a29fc7}{Fl\+\_\+\+Window\+::hide()}}. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_MOVE@{FL\_MOVE}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_MOVE@{FL\_MOVE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3acd57cae091eb27c9a52c446bdd0c164d}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3acd57cae091eb27c9a52c446bdd0c164d}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+O\+VE&The mouse has moved without any mouse buttons held down. This event is sent to the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga5b55ce634002a2743c24c4c4db7cbdd4}{Fl\+::belowmouse()}} widget.

In order to receive F\+L\+\_\+\+M\+O\+VE events, the widget must return non-\/zero when handling F\+L\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+ER. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_SHORTCUT@{FL\_SHORTCUT}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_SHORTCUT@{FL\_SHORTCUT}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a6161f0e91cc6b2947200323e3bda8156}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a6161f0e91cc6b2947200323e3bda8156}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+S\+H\+O\+R\+T\+C\+UT&If the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga7f0e9836db43268979e0b3a999583b7f}{Fl\+::focus()}} widget is zero or ignores an F\+L\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD event then F\+L\+TK tries sending this event to every widget it can, until one of them returns non-\/zero. F\+L\+\_\+\+S\+H\+O\+R\+T\+C\+UT is first sent to the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga5b55ce634002a2743c24c4c4db7cbdd4}{Fl\+::belowmouse()}} widget, then its parents and siblings, and eventually to every widget in the window, trying to find an object that returns non-\/zero. F\+L\+TK tries really hard to not to ignore any keystrokes!

You can also make \char`\"{}global\char`\"{} shortcuts by using \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__events_ga04759d795ad0df6d5ee19e82aa92b3ec}{Fl\+::add\+\_\+handler()}}. A global shortcut will work no matter what windows are displayed or which one has the focus. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_DEACTIVATE@{FL\_DEACTIVATE}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_DEACTIVATE@{FL\_DEACTIVATE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3ad9fd8e3ac1c8c3533f73205e450af9d3}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3ad9fd8e3ac1c8c3533f73205e450af9d3}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+D\+E\+A\+C\+T\+I\+V\+A\+TE&This widget is no longer active, due to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_a2eb3d2eebe8ba623c4007d4f8e66a1ee}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::deactivate()}} being called on it or one of its parents. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_ae10c2f227e76414e8142808eeda23c0c}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::active()}} may still be true after this, the widget is only active if \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_ae10c2f227e76414e8142808eeda23c0c}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::active()}} is true on it and all its parents (use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_a25ebd158cb9f7ccfa7b4cf3406c2b603}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::active\+\_\+r()}} to check this). \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_ACTIVATE@{FL\_ACTIVATE}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_ACTIVATE@{FL\_ACTIVATE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a50072421b5f3d1911d937f668d8b695d}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3a50072421b5f3d1911d937f668d8b695d}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+A\+C\+T\+I\+V\+A\+TE&This widget is now active, due to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_ae0ca5f7159aceba7d813c81167e684bb}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::activate()}} being called on it or one of its parents. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FL\_HIDE@{FL\_HIDE}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!FL\_HIDE@{FL\_HIDE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3aed9d7c8fbb9dac1e16f762195f00d5d6}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ad16daf120d9a0501cccaee563af0b9a3aed9d7c8fbb9dac1e16f762195f00d5d6}} 
F\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+DE&This widget is no longer visible, due to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_a408b7ca0d0ed7682275e79b976c5dda4}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::hide()}} being called on it or one of its parents, or due to a parent window being minimized. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_ac103c73444da9035a31329cf938d77b3}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::visible()}} may still be true after this, but the widget is visible only if visible() is true for it and all its parents (use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_ac51a7380e249127ca47aad175f162360}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::visible\+\_\+r()}} to check this). \\

F\+L\+\_\+\+S\+H\+OW&This widget is visible again, due to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_a3b7971dc3a0385c31e71b9f3786eac2d}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::show()}} being called on it or one of its parents, or due to a parent window being restored. Child Fl\+\_\+\+Windows respond to this by actually creating the window if not done already, so if you subclass a window, be sure to pass F\+L\+\_\+\+S\+H\+OW to the base class \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fl___widget_a3521aba25eda761620953dd49d335ea7}{Fl\+\_\+\+Widget\+::handle()}} method! \\

F\+L\+\_\+\+P\+A\+S\+TE&You should get this event some time after you call \mbox{\hyperlink{group__fl__clipboard_ga0f30d10ec79056fbdbf8d2f4dca4d565}{Fl\+::paste()}}. The labeltype() method sets the type of the label.

The following standard label types are included\+:

Get the filled version of a frame. If no filled version of a given frame exists, the behavior of this function is undefined and some random box or frame is returned. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_ae421f6f475053ece0a0dd80e9198ac07}\label{_enumerations_8_h_ae421f6f475053ece0a0dd80e9198ac07}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_a2f613709d1c9444f9f03e7c0349223f3}\label{_enumerations_8_h_a2f613709d1c9444f9f03e7c0349223f3}} 
\index{Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}!fl\_color\_cube@{fl\_color\_cube}}
\index{fl\_color\_cube@{fl\_color\_cube}!Enumerations.H@{Enumerations.H}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{fl\_color\_cube()}{fl\_color\_cube()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a8b762953646f8abee866061f1af78a6a}{Fl\+\_\+\+Color}} fl\+\_\+color\+\_\+cube (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{r,  }\item[{int}]{g,  }\item[{int}]{b }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Returns a color out of the color cube.

{\ttfamily r} must be in the range 0 to F\+L\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+R\+ED (5) minus 1, {\ttfamily g} must be in the range 0 to F\+L\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+E\+EN (8) minus 1, {\ttfamily b} must be in the range 0 to F\+L\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+B\+L\+UE (5) minus 1.

To get the closest color to a 8-\/bit set of R,G,B values use\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a2f613709d1c9444f9f03e7c0349223f3}{fl\_color\_cube}}(R * (\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a696105c253ebbfd89d9dfc37357ed728}{FL\_NUM\_RED}} -\/ 1) / 255,}
\DoxyCodeLine{   G * (\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_aff583e05dea4ac7ec09c3f1760a503c0}{FL\_NUM\_GREEN}} -\/ 1) / 255,}
\DoxyCodeLine{   B * (\mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a35ff0c922707d57042cd509c88f88fea}{FL\_NUM\_BLUE}} -\/ 1) / 255);}
\end{DoxyCode}
 \mbox{\Hypertarget{_enumerations_8_h_a4f5d2c8d4113f0af892f9ba232b24ec6}\label{_enumerations_8_h_a4f5d2c8d4113f0af892f9ba232b24ec6}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_enumerations_8_h_a8b762953646f8abee866061f1af78a6a}{Fl\+\_\+\+Color}} fl\+\_\+gray\+\_\+ramp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{i }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Returns a gray color value from black (i == 0) to white (i == F\+L\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+AY -\/ 1). F\+L\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+AY is defined to be 24 in the current F\+L\+TK release. To get the closest F\+L\+TK gray value to an 8-\/bit grayscale color \textquotesingle{}I\textquotesingle{} use\+:
